# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="5918e-102">Membros obsoletos no .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5918e-102">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5918e-103">Este artigo lista os membros do tipo que estão obsoletos no .NET Framework 4.5 e nas versões posteriores.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5918e-103">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5918e-104">Os membros do tipo são agrupados por montagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5918e-104">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="5918e-105">Este artigo não lista os membros de tipos obsoletos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5918e-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="5918e-106">Para obter uma lista de tipos obsoletos, consulte [tipos obsoletos](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="5918e-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>
